# See ES_plugin_script_galactic_capital_investment.py for the code that generates this script.

mission "gci init"
	non-blocking
	invisible
	landing
	repeat
	to offer
		or
			"stock value Delta V = 0"
			not "gci init: failed"
	on offer
		lastvisit = "days since start"
		"stock last day" = "days since start"
		"stock value Southbound Shipyards" = 1322
		"sb_anchor_monthly" = 1322
		"stock amount Southbound Shipyards" = 0
		"sb_avg_price" = 0
		"sb_daily_notional_volume" = 0
		"stock value Lionheart Shipyards" = 976
		"li_anchor_monthly" = 976
		"stock amount Lionheart Shipyards" = 0
		"li_avg_price" = 0
		"li_daily_notional_volume" = 0
		"stock value Megaparsec Shipyards" = 1110
		"me_anchor_monthly" = 1110
		"stock amount Megaparsec Shipyards" = 0
		"me_avg_price" = 0
		"me_daily_notional_volume" = 0
		"stock value Syndicate Shipyards" = 1692
		"sy_anchor_monthly" = 1692
		"stock amount Syndicate Shipyards" = 0
		"sy_avg_price" = 0
		"sy_daily_notional_volume" = 0
		"stock value Kraz Cybernetics" = 1451
		"kz_anchor_monthly" = 1451
		"stock amount Kraz Cybernetics" = 0
		"kz_avg_price" = 0
		"kz_daily_notional_volume" = 0
		"stock value Deep Sky" = 837
		"ds_anchor_monthly" = 837
		"stock amount Deep Sky" = 0
		"ds_avg_price" = 0
		"ds_daily_notional_volume" = 0
		"stock value Lovelace Labs" = 1791
		"ll_anchor_monthly" = 1791
		"stock amount Lovelace Labs" = 0
		"ll_avg_price" = 0

		"dv_anchor_monthly" = 788
		"stock amount Delta V" = 0
		"dv_avg_price" = 0
		"dv_daily_notional_volume" = 0
		"stock value Betelgeuse Shipyards" = 1224
		"be_anchor_monthly" = 1224
		"stock amount Betelgeuse Shipyards" = 0

mission "gci banking account update"
	non-blocking
	invisible
	repeat
	landing
	to offer
		has "gci init: failed"
	on offer
		datedifference = "days since start" - lastvisit
		lastvisit = "days since start"
		dailyincome = deposit * 149 / 100000 - "salary: Galactic Capital Transfer"
		deposit += datedifference * dailyincome
		fail

mission "gci stock dividends"
	entering
	invisible
	repeat
	non-blocking
	destination "Earth"
	to offer
		"day" == 1
		or
			"stock amount Southbound Shipyards" > 0
			"stock amount Syndicate Shipyards" > 0
			"stock amount Kraz Cybernetics" > 0
			"stock amount Lovelace Labs" > 0
			"stock amount Betelgeuse Shipyards" > 0

	on offer
		conversation
			label "start"
			action
				"passed days" = "days since start" - "stock last day"
			``
			label "days loop"
			branch "end"
				"passed days" == 0
			action
				"stock roll Southbound Shipyards" = "roll: 100"
				"stock multiplier Southbound Shipyards" = 10200
			branch "dividend roll 1 Southbound Shipyards"
				"stock roll Southbound Shipyards" == 1
			branch "dividend roll 2 Southbound Shipyards"
				"stock roll Southbound Shipyards" <= 7
			branch "dividend roll 3 Southbound Shipyards"
				"stock roll Southbound Shipyards" <= 22
			branch "dividend roll 4 Southbound Shipyards"
				"stock roll Southbound Shipyards" <= 45
			branch "dividend roll 5 Southbound Shipyards"
				"stock roll Southbound Shipyards" <= 88
			branch "apply Southbound Shipyards"
			label "dividend roll 1 Southbound Shipyards"
			action
				"stock multiplier Southbound Shipyards" = 8874
			branch "apply Southbound Shipyards"
			label "dividend roll 2 Southbound Shipyards"
			action
				"stock multiplier Southbound Shipyards" = 9800
			branch "apply Southbound Shipyards"
			label "dividend roll 3 Southbound Shipyards"
			action

			branch "apply Southbound Shipyards"

				"stock all dividends" = "stock dividends addi"

			label "dividends payment 1000000000"
			branch "dividends payment 100000000"

				payment 1000000000
				"stock dividends addi" -= 1000000000

				payment 100000000
				"stock dividends addi" -= 100000000
			branch "dividends payment 100000000"

			label "dividends payment 10000000"
			branch "dividends payment 1000000"
				"stock dividends addi" < 10000000
			action
				payment 10000000
				"stock dividends addi" -= 10000000
			branch "dividends payment 10000000"

			label "dividends payment 1000000"
			branch "dividends payment 100000"
				"stock dividends addi" < 1000000
			action
				payment 1000000
				"stock dividends addi" -= 1000000
			branch "dividends payment 1000000"

			label "dividends payment 100000"
			branch "dividends payment 10000"
				"stock dividends addi" < 100000
			action
				payment 100000
				"stock dividends addi" -= 100000
			branch "dividends payment 100000"

			label "dividends payment 10000"
			branch "dividends payment 1000"
				"stock dividends addi" < 10000
			action
				payment 10000
				"stock dividends addi" -= 10000
			branch "dividends payment 10000"

			label "dividends payment 1000"
			branch "dividends payment 100"
				"stock dividends addi" < 1000
			action
				payment 1000
				"stock dividends addi" -= 1000
			branch "dividends payment 1000"

			label "dividends payment 100"
			branch "dividends payment 10"
				"stock dividends addi" < 100
			action
				payment 100
				"stock dividends addi" -= 100
			branch "dividends payment 100"

			label "dividends payment 10"
			branch "dividends payment 1"
				"stock dividends addi" < 10
			action
				payment 10
				"stock dividends addi" -= 10
			branch "dividends payment 10"

			label "dividends payment 1"
			branch "dividends payment done"
				"stock dividends addi" < 1
			action
				payment 1
				"stock dividends addi" -= 1
			branch "dividends payment 1"


			label "dividends payment done"
			scene "scene/stock_chart_analysis"
			`This is your monthly stock report and dividend payout.`
			`You hold &[stock amount Southbound Shipyards] "Southbound Shipyards" stocks at &[stock value Southbound Shipyards] credits each. Monthly dividend (1.22%): &[dividend Southbound Shipyards]`
				to display
					"stock amount Southbound Shipyards" > 0
			`You hold &[stock amount Lionheart Shipyards] "Lionheart Shipyards" stocks at &[stock value Lionheart Shipyards] credits each. Monthly dividend (0%): &[dividend Lionheart Shipyards]`
				to display
					"stock amount Lionheart Shipyards" > 0
			`You hold &[stock amount Megaparsec Shipyards] "Megaparsec Shipyards" stocks at &[stock value Megaparsec Shipyards] credits each. Monthly dividend (0%): &[dividend Megaparsec Shipyards]`
				to display
					"stock amount Megaparsec Shipyards" > 0
			`You hold &[stock amount Syndicate Shipyards] "Syndicate Shipyards" stocks at &[stock value Syndicate Shipyards] credits each. Monthly dividend (1.22%): &[dividend Syndicate Shipyards]`
				to display
					"stock amount Syndicate Shipyards" > 0
			`You hold &[stock amount Kraz Cybernetics] "Kraz Cybernetics" stocks at &[stock value Kraz Cybernetics] credits each. Monthly dividend (1.22%): &[dividend Kraz Cybernetics]`
				to display
					"stock amount Kraz Cybernetics" > 0
			`You hold &[stock amount Deep Sky] "Deep Sky" stocks at &[stock value Deep Sky] credits each. Monthly dividend (0%): &[dividend Deep Sky]`
				to display
					"stock amount Deep Sky" > 0
			`You hold &[stock amount Lovelace Labs] "Lovelace Labs" stocks at &[stock value Lovelace Labs] credits each. Monthly dividend (1.22%): &[dividend Lovelace Labs]`
				to display
					"stock amount Lovelace Labs" > 0
			`You hold &[stock amount Delta V] "Delta V" stocks at &[stock value Delta V] credits each. Monthly dividend (0%): &[dividend Delta V]`
				to display
					"stock amount Delta V" > 0
			`You hold &[stock amount Betelgeuse Shipyards] "Betelgeuse Shipyards" stocks at &[stock value Betelgeuse Shipyards] credits each. Monthly dividend (1.22%): &[dividend Betelgeuse Shipyards]`
				to display
					"stock amount Betelgeuse Shipyards" > 0
			`You hold &[stock amount Tarazed Corporation] "Tarazed Corporation" stocks at &[stock value Tarazed Corporation] credits each. Monthly dividend (0%): &[dividend Tarazed Corporation]`
				to display
					"stock amount Tarazed Corporation" > 0

			``
			`All dividend payouts: &[stock all dividends]`
				decline

				"li_cost_basis" = "li_avg_price" * "stock amount Lionheart Shipyards"
				"total_principal" += "li_cost_basis"
				"me_cost_basis" = "me_avg_price" * "stock amount Megaparsec Shipyards"
				"total_principal" += "me_cost_basis"
				"sy_cost_basis" = "sy_avg_price" * "stock amount Syndicate Shipyards"
				"total_principal" += "sy_cost_basis"
				"kz_cost_basis" = "kz_avg_price" * "stock amount Kraz Cybernetics"
				"total_principal" += "kz_cost_basis"
				"ds_cost_basis" = "ds_avg_price" * "stock amount Deep Sky"
				"total_principal" += "ds_cost_basis"
				"ll_cost_basis" = "ll_avg_price" * "stock amount Lovelace Labs"
				"total_principal" += "ll_cost_basis"
				"dv_cost_basis" = "dv_avg_price" * "stock amount Delta V"
				"total_principal" += "dv_cost_basis"
				"be_cost_basis" = "be_avg_price" * "stock amount Betelgeuse Shipyards"
				"total_principal" += "be_cost_basis"
				"ta_cost_basis" = "ta_avg_price" * "stock amount Tarazed Corporation"
				"total_principal" += "ta_cost_basis"

				"current_val_total" = "stocktotalvalue"
			branch "calc total roi"
				"total_principal" > 0
			action
				"total_up_alltime" = 0
			branch "calc total roi end"
			label "calc total roi"
			action
				"total_roi" = "current_val_total" * 100 / "total_principal"
				"total_up_alltime" = "total_roi" - 100
			label "calc total roi end"

			`Welcome to "Galactic Capital Investment Service"! Your last visit is &[datedifference] day/s ago.`
			``
			`Cash chip balance:`
			`	&[credits] credits`
			`Savings account balance:`
			`	&[deposit] credits`
			`	&[dailyincome] credits daily interest + &[salary: Galactic Capital Transfer] credits daily cash withdrawals`
			``
			`Daily investment salary to your cash chip: &[salary: GCI Private Markets] credits`
			`Stock Portfolio value: &[stocktotalvalue] credits (up &[total_up_alltime]% all-time)`
			`Family trust: &[global: familytrust] credits (0% monthly, for all pilots)`
			``
			choice
				`	[access to your savings account]`
					goto linebankaccount
				`	[access to your family trust]`
					goto linefamilytrust
				`	[access to your daily cash withdrawal]`
					goto linecashtransfer
				`	[access to the stock exchange]`
					goto linestockexchange
				`	[sell investments]`
					to display
						"salary: Galactic Capital" > 0
					goto linesellinvestment
				`	[enable GCI missions and private investments]`
					to display
						not "global: gcijobs active"
					goto setjobs1
				`	[disable GCI missions and private investments]`
					to display
						has "global: gcijobs active"
					goto setjobs0
				`	[leave]`
					goto end

			label linebankaccount
			``

			branch "sell stocks 100 Tarazed Corporation"
			label "sell stocks 10 Tarazed Corporation"
			branch "sell stocks 1 Tarazed Corporation"
				"waterfall_cost" < 10
			action
				payment 10
				"waterfall_cost" -= 10
			branch "sell stocks 10 Tarazed Corporation"
			label "sell stocks 1 Tarazed Corporation"
			branch "sell stocks end Tarazed Corporation"
				"waterfall_cost" < 1
			action
				payment 1
				"waterfall_cost" -= 1
			branch "sell stocks 1 Tarazed Corporation"
			label "sell stocks end Tarazed Corporation"
			branch "Sell Tarazed Corporation"



			label setjobs0
			action
				clear "global: gcijobs active"
			`Job board investments/missions are hidden now.`
				goto menu
			label setjobs1
			action
				set "global: gcijobs active"
			`Job board investments/missions are shown now.`
				goto menu

			label clearscreen
			``
				goto menu
			label end
			``
			scene scene/gci_terminal
			`Thank you for being a valued customer at Galactic Capital Investments!`
				decline
		fail
